msg:My husband and I were on a part-time trip this time, so we booked a room on the platform in a hurry without high expectations. But upon arrival there were a series of unexpected surprises. In the National Wetland Reserve, the air is fresh, the scenery is beautiful, and there are rich natural species (I saw non-toxic green spiders for the first time). The Hong Kong-style tension immediately relaxed. No wonder Song Gaozong "considered Hangzhou as Bianzhou" .
When we checked in, several staff at the front desk (Jeniffer, Nicole, Frank) were very helpful. Although they had prepared a room for us in advance, when they knew we were bringing children, they took the initiative to provide room information and patiently allowed us to return. Choose the most convenient location and happily take us to see several types of rooms until we are satisfied. After that, the concierge was immediately arranged to quickly transport our luggage to the room. The housekeeping depar**ent also immediately sent rich fruits and Western snacks to the room, and lit soothing aromatherapy essential oil. The most considerate thing was to light mosquito coils. The room was mosquito-free and the air-conditioning was sufficient. . Front desk leadership colleagues demonstrate excellent coordination and organizational skills.
The mattress is the best among the 5-star hotels I have ever been to. The pillows and quilt are also very comfortable, so I can sleep soundly all night long (especially better than at homeü§≠). The housekeeper thoughtfully asked us how much bottled water we needed and where special cleaning was needed, so that we could safely accommodate our children.
Baiyun Restaurant really surprised me the most. The ingredients are fresh and the cooking oil is not reused. Even my glass belly was completely fine after eating it. What I didn‚Äôt expect was that the West Lake Vinegar Fish is the best I‚Äôve ever had in the past twenty years. The best in the restaurant, the chef is so patient and uses enough aged vinegar to make a juice that is unimaginably delicious and hangs it on the freshly slaughtered mandarin fish. It is heavenly delicious! Absolutely amazing! I hope that after my top secret is revealed, visitors will not visit Baiyun Restaurant. Besides, they also have other special dishes, which I am sorry I cannot tell you one by one. The surprise of the Western restaurant is that the young chef cooks authentic curries. Even healthy and light Western dishes such as mixed vegetable soup and steamed cod can bring out their original flavors and make people linger aftertaste. A large number of vegetables can actually be mixed to create natural The sweetness of the fusion made me look at the domestic Western cuisine with admiration and admiration.
We have stayed at Banyan Tree hotels in various places in the past, and they all have their own characteristics. The only thing that remains constant is the considerate way they treat guests like family. The colleagues at Hangzhou Branch are gentle, courteous, and quick to act. This is a place we will definitely visit again!

msg:The first time I stayed in a Banyan Tree hotel, Xixi gave me a big surprise. Because I had booked a Qingming holiday to Guilin early, and when I confirmed that it would rain there the day before departure, I changed my itinerary temporarily and wanted to go to Hangzhou, but I found that there were not many hotels to choose from. I blindly chose Banyan Tree based on the luxury list. I chose its villa on the first day, and a suite for the next two nights. In contrast, the suite is much better. In addition to the new equipment, the room is also large enough. There are two bathrooms, one of which is equipped with a smart toilet, which is much better than the villa. Moreover, the sofa in the living room can be turned into a super large double bed. Two double beds are really comfortable for a family of three. In addition, the lighting and air conditioning control systems in the room are simple, reasonable and user-friendly. The family had a very high quality of sleep in the suite for these two nights. In the morning, I opened the curtains, looked at the lake view outside, and listened to the chirping of birds. Well, this is what a luxury resort hotel should feel like. The overall architectural style of the hotel also complements the misty April in the south of the Yangtze River. What's more, there is a world-renowned wetland park next to it. This unique geographical location deserves the comment of excellence. In addition, the weather is also great. It basically didn't rain when I went out to play. It was even more rare that I encountered a sunny sky for most of the day. It was really a perfect holiday. There are many factors that add icing on the cake. On the first night in the villa, I woke up early and saw squirrels on the tree on the balcony. The children were very surprised; the package I bought included a free one-hour travel photo shoot, and my wife enjoyed it very much; the hotel provided a customized one-day tour of West Lake, which made my family who had never been to Hangzhou satisfied. Of course, there is also their service. Every staff member I met, the uncle from the tourism depar**ent, Viola, Finley, and Nicole at the front desk, are responsive and respond very quickly. When I came back from the wetland park, it was raining. I made a phone call and they immediately drove a battery car to pick me up. I have stayed in many expensive hotels. I think the service is really good. Banyan Tree Xixi is one of the best.
If I have to say what is not perfect, I think it is the hotel's catering. The breakfast is OK, the variety is not very large, but the Chinese and Western food including local specialties are still very delicious. There are too few restaurants in the hotel, and the Chinese restaurant is relatively small. The quality of the dishes is very good, but it is not easy to reserve a table. In addition, the remaining Western restaurants are hard to describe. When it was past 7 o'clock in the evening, it was deserted and there was no customer. I think this is probably related to its dishes and cost-effectiveness. If the Chinese restaurant can score 8 points for food taste, the Western restaurant can only score 5 points at most. I hope the hotel can focus on improving the quality of the Western restaurant, so that more guests can choose to dine in the hotel and improve their experience.
